--
-- Name: add_doctor(text, integer, character varying); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.add_doctor("docName" text, exp integer, spec character varying) RETURNS void
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $_$begin
	insert into doctor (doctor_name,work_experience,spec_name ) values($1,$2,$3);
EXCEPTION
WHEN unique_violation THEN
	RAISE NOTICE 'Уже есть';
end$_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.add_doctor("docName" text, exp integer, spec character varying) OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- Name: add_patient(text, integer, text, text, text, integer); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.add_patient("patName" text, "patAge" integer, "patGender" text, "docName" text, "ilnessName" text, "wardNumber" integer) RETURNS void
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $_$declare
	tmp text;
begin
insert into patient (patient_name,age,gender,ward) values ($1,$2,$3,$6);
select appoint_doctor($1,$4) into tmp;
select appoint_ilness($5,$1) into tmp;
EXCEPTION
WHEN unique_violation THEN
	RAISE NOTICE 'Уже есть';
return;
end$_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.add_patient("patName" text, "patAge" integer, "patGender" text, "docName" text, "ilnessName" text, "wardNumber" integer) OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- Name: appoint_doctor(integer, integer); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.appoint_doctor(integer, integer) RETURNS void
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $_$begin
insert into patient_doctor (patient_patient_id,doctor_doctor_id) values ($1,$2);
EXCEPTION
WHEN unique_violation THEN
	RAISE NOTICE 'Уже есть';
end$_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.appoint_doctor(integer, integer) OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- Name: appoint_doctor(text, text); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.appoint_doctor("patName" text, "docName" text) RETURNS void
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $_$declare 
pat_id integer;
doc_id integer;
begin
doc_id := (select doctor_id from doctor where doctor_name = $2 limit 1);
pat_id := (select patient_id from patient where patient_name = $1 limit 1);
insert into patient_doctor (patient_patient_id, doctor_doctor_id) values (pat_id,doc_id);
EXCEPTION
WHEN unique_violation THEN
	RAISE NOTICE 'Уже есть';
	return;
end;$_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.appoint_doctor("patName" text, "docName" text) OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- Name: appoint_ilness(integer, integer); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.appoint_ilness(integer, integer) RETURNS void
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $_$begin
insert into patient_ilness (patient_patient_id, ilness_ilness_id) values ($1,$2);
EXCEPTION
WHEN unique_violation THEN
	RAISE NOTICE 'Уже есть';
end$_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.appoint_ilness(integer, integer) OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- Name: appoint_ilness(text, text); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.appoint_ilness("ilnessName" text, "patName" text) RETURNS void
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $_$declare
iln_id integer;
pat_id integer;
begin
	iln_id := (select ilness_id from ilness where ilness_name = $1 limit 1);
	pat_id := (select patient_id from patient where patient_name = $2 limit 1);
	insert into patient_ilness (ilness_ilness_id,patient_patient_id) values (iln_id, pat_id);
	EXCEPTION
	WHEN unique_violation THEN
		RAISE NOTICE 'Уже есть';
	return;
end;$_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.appoint_ilness("ilnessName" text, "patName" text) OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- Name: ch_cap(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.ch_cap() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
begin
raise notice '%',NEW.patient_name;
if (select capacity from wards where wards.number = NEW.ward limit 1) <=  count(*) from get_ward_info(NEW.ward) then
	raise notice 'mest net';
	NEW.ward := (select wards.number from wards where wards.capacity > (select count(*) from get_ward_info(wards.number)) limit 1);
else
	raise notice 'naznachil palaty';
end if;
return NEW;
end
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.ch_cap() OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- Name: change_encrypt_clients(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: admin1
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.change_encrypt_clients() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
DECLARE
	encrypt_username TEXT;
	encrypt_key_user TEXT;
	new_key_user TEXT;
BEGIN
	SELECT keyUser INTO new_key_user FROM user_key WHERE username=current_user;
	IF TG_OP='INSERT' THEN 
		NEW.password := pgp_sym_encrypt(NEW.password, new_key_user);
		--INSERT INTO last_change VALUES (NEW.user_id, current_user);
	END IF;
	IF TG_OP='UPDATE' THEN
		SELECT username INTO encrypt_username FROM last_change WHERE user_id = OLD.client_id;
		SELECT keyUser INTO encrypt_key_user FROM user_key WHERE username=encrypt_username;
		IF NEW.password = OLD.password THEN
			NEW.password := pgp_sym_decrypt(old.password::bytea,encrypt_key_user);
		END IF;
		
		NEW.password := pgp_sym_encrypt(NEW.password , new_key_user);
		UPDATE last_change SET user_id = NEW.user_id, username=current_user WHERE user_id = OLD.user_id;
	END IF;
RETURN NEW;
END
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.change_encrypt_clients() OWNER TO admin1;

--
-- Name: check_index(integer); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.check_index(p_count integer) RETURNS numeric
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
DECLARE
	PK Integer;
	start_time timestamp;
	end_time timestamp;
	average_time numeric(14,8) := 0;
BEGIN
	FOR i IN 1..p_count LOOP
		start_time := clock_timestamp();
		PK := RANDOM() * 5000 + 17000 AS INTEGER;
		EXECUTE format('SELECT * FROM patient WHERE patient_id = %L', PK);
		end_time := clock_timestamp();
		average_time := average_time + extract(EPOCH from end_time - start_time);
	END LOOP;
																 
	average_time := average_time / p_count;															 
	
	RAISE NOTICE 'Среднее время выполнения запроса: %', average_time;
	RETURN average_time;
END;
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.check_index(p_count integer) OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- Name: decrypt_clients(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: admin1
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.decrypt_clients() RETURNS TABLE(username text, password text)
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
DECLARE
    r RECORD;
BEGIN
    FOR r IN SELECT *  FROM cred
	LOOP
		RETURN QUERY VALUES (r.username, pgp_sym_decrypt(r.password::bytea, (SELECT keyUser FROM user_key WHERE user_key.username='admin1')));
	END LOOP;
	RETURN;
END;
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.decrypt_clients() OWNER TO admin1;

--
-- Name: delete_creds(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: admin1
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.delete_creds() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
BEGIN
	IF TG_OP='DELETE' THEN
		DELETE FROM last_change WHERE user_id = OLD.user_id;
	END IF;
	IF TG_OP='TRUNCATE' THEN
		TRUNCATE TABLE last_change;
	END IF;
RETURN NULL;
END
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.delete_creds() OWNER TO admin1;

--
-- Name: get_doc_info(text); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.get_doc_info(pat_name text) RETURNS SETOF public.docinfo
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $_$
declare
	tmp docinfo;
begin
		if  $1 = 'Введите фамилию доктора' then
			$1 = '';
		end if;
		for tmp.doc_name,tmp.exp,tmp.spec,tmp.pat_name in (select doctor.doctor_name,doctor.work_experience,doctor.spec_name,patient.patient_name from (doctor left join patient_doctor on doctor_id=doctor_doctor_id ) left join patient on patient_patient_id = patient_id where doctor_name ilike $1 || '%')
		loop
			return next tmp;
		end loop;
		return;
end
$_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.get_doc_info(pat_name text) OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- Name: get_pat_info(text); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.get_pat_info(pat_name text) RETURNS SETOF public.patinfo
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $_$declare
	tmp patinfo;
	c bool;
begin
		if  $1 = 'Введите фамилию пациента' then
			$1 = '';
		end if;
		for tmp.patname,tmp.patage,tmp.patgender,tmp.ward,tmp.docname,tmp.ilnessname in (select patient.patient_name,patient.age,patient.gender,patient.ward,doctor.doctor_name,ilness.ilness_name from ((((patient left join patient_doctor on patient_id=patient_patient_id ) left join doctor on doctor_doctor_id = doctor_id) left join patient_ilness on patient_ilness.patient_patient_id=patient_id) left join ilness on ilness_id=ilness_ilness_id) where patient_name ilike $1 || '%')
		loop
			return next tmp;
		end loop;
		return;
end$_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.get_pat_info(pat_name text) OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- Name: get_ward_info(integer); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.get_ward_info(integer) RETURNS TABLE(pat_name character varying)
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $_$
begin
	return query select patient_name from patient  where ward = $1 FOR UPDATE;
end
$_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.get_ward_info(integer) OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- Name: insert_log(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: admin1
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.insert_log() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
BEGIN
		IF TG_OP='INSERT' THEN 
			INSERT INTO log VALUES (NEXTVAL('id_log'), session_user, TG_OP, TG_TABLE_NAME, current_timestamp,NULL,NEW::text);
		END IF;
		IF TG_OP='UPDATE' THEN
			INSERT INTO log VALUES (NEXTVAL('id_log'), session_user, TG_OP, TG_TABLE_NAME, current_timestamp,OLD::text,NEW::text);
		END IF;
		IF TG_OP='DELETE' THEN
			INSERT INTO log VALUES (NEXTVAL('id_log'), session_user, TG_OP, TG_TABLE_NAME, current_timestamp,OLD::text,NULL);
		END IF;
		IF TG_OP='TRUNCATE' THEN
			INSERT INTO log VALUES (NEXTVAL('id_log'), session_user, TG_OP, TG_TABLE_NAME, current_timestamp,NULL,NULL);
		END IF;
RETURN NULL;
END
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.insert_log() OWNER TO admin1;

--
-- Name: insert_log_ddl(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: admin1
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.insert_log_ddl() RETURNS event_trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
DECLARE
  r RECORD;
BEGIN
  IF tg_tag <> 'DROP TABLE' THEN
    FOR r IN SELECT * FROM pg_event_trigger_ddl_commands()
	LOOP
		INSERT INTO log_ddl VALUES (NEXTVAL('id_log_ddl'), current_timestamp, r.command_tag, r.object_identity, current_user);
	END LOOP;
  END IF;
END;
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.insert_log_ddl() OWNER TO admin1;

--
-- Name: insert_log_ddl_drop(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: admin1
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.insert_log_ddl_drop() RETURNS event_trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
DECLARE
  r RECORD;
BEGIN
    FOR r IN SELECT * FROM pg_event_trigger_dropped_objects() 
    LOOP
      INSERT INTO log_ddl VALUES (NEXTVAL('id_log_ddl'), current_timestamp, tg_tag, r.object_identity, current_user);
	END LOOP;
END;
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.insert_log_ddl_drop() OWNER TO admin1;

--
-- Name: login(text, text); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.login(username text, password text) RETURNS boolean
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $_$begin
	if $2 = (select cred.password from cred where cred.username=$1) then
		return true;
	else
		return false;
	end if;
end$_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.login(username text, password text) OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- Name: doctor; Type: TABLE; Schema: public; Owner: admin
--

CREATE TABLE public.doctor (
    doctor_id integer NOT NULL,
    doctor_name character varying(100) NOT NULL,
    work_experience integer NOT NULL,
    spec_name character varying(100) NOT NULL
);


ALTER TABLE public.doctor OWNER TO admin;

--
-- Name: doctor_doctor_id_seq; Type: SEQUENCE; Schema: public; Owner: admin
--

ALTER TABLE public.doctor ALTER COLUMN doctor_id ADD GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY (
    SEQUENCE NAME public.doctor_doctor_id_seq
    START WITH 1
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NO MINVALUE
    NO MAXVALUE
    CACHE 1
);

--
-- Name: patient doctorrls; Type: POLICY; Schema: public; Owner: admin
--

CREATE POLICY doctorrls ON public.patient TO maindoctor USING ((patient_id IN ( SELECT patient_doctor.patient_patient_id
   FROM public.patient_doctor
  WHERE (patient_doctor.doctor_doctor_id IN ( SELECT doctor.doctor_id
           FROM public.doctor
          WHERE ((doctor.doctor_name)::text ~~* (CURRENT_USER)::text))))));

--
-- Name: user_key encryptpatient; Type: POLICY; Schema: public; Owner: admin1
--

CREATE POLICY encryptpatient ON public.user_key TO maindoctor, patient USING (((username = CURRENT_USER) OR (username IN ( SELECT last_change.username
   FROM public.last_change))));
